 Shaanxi Huaxi"  

### Key Notes:  
- **Shaanxi (陕西)**: Refers to the Chinese province (spelled with a double "a" to differentiate from *Shanxi* 山西).  
- **Huaxi (华西)**: The name of the pharmaceutical manufacturer.  
- **Xiaoaiping Syrup (消癌平糖浆)**: A traditional Chinese medicine (TCM) syrup used adjunctively in cancer management. The name combines "消癌" (cancer-suppressing) and "平" (stabilizing/calming).  

The repeated "Shaanxi Huaxi" emphasizes the product's origin and manufacturer.  

---  
**Optional Additions (if needed):**  
1. **Usage**: Often integrated into TCM regimens to alleviate side effects of conventional treatments or inhibit tumor growth.  
2. **Composition**: Typically contains herbal extracts like *Solamum nigrum* (白英) or other antitumor ingredients.
